        var loyalUserCookie = 'loyal-user';
        if (Cookies.get(loyalUserCookie)) {
            var cookieData = Cookies.getJSON(loyalUserCookie);
            if (!cookieData.isLoyal) {
                var diff = new Date() - Date.parse(cookieData.date);
                var diffInMinutes = Math.round(((diff % 86400000) % 3600000) / 60000);
                if (diffInMinutes > 20) {
                    window.gtag("event", "loyal-user", {
                        event_category: "micro-conversion",
                        event_label: "visit-homepage",
                    })
                    cookieData.isLoyal = true;
                    Cookies.set(loyalUserCookie, cookieData);
                }
            }
        }
        if (!Cookies.get(loyalUserCookie)) {
            var data = { date: new Date(), isLoyal: false };
            Cookies.set(loyalUserCookie, data, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
        }
    </script>

<script>
      (function () {
        window.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
          renderLoginIframe('/silent-login/')
        });
        window.addEventListener("message", handleLoginMessage);
        function handleLoginMessage(msg) {
          if (msg.data.kind !== 'SilentLoginResult' || msg.origin !== window.location.origin) return;
          document.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent("__silent_login__", { detail: msg.data }));
        }
        function renderLoginIframe(src) {
          var iframe = document.createElement("iframe");
          iframe.src = src;
          iframe.style = "display: none !important";
          iframe.setAttribute("aria-hidden", true);
          document.body.appendChild(iframe);
        }
      })();
    </script>
